if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '2f6f66429fb5f59eda2856eb475b6ac2b9246554') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2f6f66429fb5f59eda2856eb475b6ac2b9246554') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'cf230c7ed620334c2a5d9709fc83a9b755528759') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2f6f66429fb5f59eda2856eb475b6ac2b9246554') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/setup_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup_base.js');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup_base.js') != 'f0775aa0c58b4a9955fe80e349da2227d14c844b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup_base.js') !== 'f0775aa0c58b4a9955fe80e349da2227d14c844b') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup_base.js') !== '1bc1d090cf90d850005906e8a2accfe1f4f289f8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup_base.js') !== 'f0775aa0c58b4a9955fe80e349da2227d14c844b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup_base.js');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 363\n");

echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
